{"id":"8128823a-e372-42aa-9e64-acc0585ab0f1","identifier":"FRG-229","title":"Bug: Stale slot reservations — objects stay 'full' after character leaves","description":"## Problem

QA confirmed: objects show 'full' (occupied pip) permanently after characters finish interacting and leave. Stove showed 'full' for 8+ sim hours with no character present. Reproduced on stove, desk, easel, fridge, bonsai. Only Reset clears the stale slots.

## Evidence

* Stove: full from 2:40 PM onwards, no character at stove. Persisted until Reset.
* After Reset: Nyx used stove \\~10:12 AM, stove shows full at 1:46 PM with no character present.
* Bonsai: showed full for hours, eventually freed inconsistently.

## Root Cause

The interaction-end detection in Engine.js (line 108) checks prevAction === 'interacting' && char.action !== 'interacting' && prevInteractTarget, then calls objectEngine.release(). This SHOULD work but QA shows it doesn't reliably fire.

Possible causes:

1. The prevAction/prevInteractTarget capture (line 67-68) and char.update() (line 105) have a race — if something else changes the action between capture and check
2. arrive() is called with [char.name](<http://char.name>) but release() might use a different identifier
3. \\_handleObjectArrival clears targetObjectId before startInteraction — ordering issue with the detection
4. The object's auto_next timer might reset the state (and clear the interaction) BEFORE the character's interactTimer expires, breaking the detection

## Fix

Add defensive release: when a character transitions out of interacting (in Character.js or Engine.js), always release the slot. Add console.warn for any release on an unknown occupant to catch orphaned slots.

## Acceptance Criteria

* Objects return to correct free count after character finishes interaction
* No stale full pips after 10+ sim hours
* QA re-verification passes","projectMilestone":{"id":"d98e487a-66f2-4106-86d3-550aac4cb898","name":"M1: Sim engine correct (debug foundation)"},"priority":{"value":1,"name":"Urgent"},"url":"https://linear.app/chills-linear/issue/FRG-229/bug-stale-slot-reservations-objects-stay-full-after-character-leaves","gitBranchName":"chillkimtest/frg-229-bug-stale-slot-reservations-objects-stay-full-after","createdAt":"2026-03-07T22:12:41.381Z","updatedAt":"2026-03-07T22:12:41.381Z","archivedAt":null,"completedAt":null,"dueDate":null,"slaStartedAt":null,"slaMediumRiskAt":null,"slaHighRiskAt":null,"slaBreachesAt":null,"slaType":"all","status":"Todo","labels":[],"attachments":[],"documents":[],"createdBy":"Chill","createdById":"b5a6e03a-2da1-4e78-951b-81497e2a00f7","project":"AI Aquarium","projectId":"0385a8c7-ba5a-43a3-b223-acf4d1ad6d63","team":"Forge","teamId":"c3ef97d8-21a8-4aa7-a818-298f217864dd"}

USERMESSAGE #13
✓ TOOL RESULT
SUCCESS 
     1→/**
     2→ * Engine.js — SimulationEngine: manages characters, object state machines, and
     3→ * default random-wander behaviour (with 30% chance of object interaction).
     4→ */
     5→
     6→import { ObjectEngine, OBJECT_DEFS } from './objects.js';
     7→
     8→export class SimulationEngine {
     9→  /**
    10→   * @param {object}      config
    11→   * @param {boolean[][]} config.walkable   - walkable[row][col]
    12→   * @param {number}      config.gridCols
    13→   * @param {number}      config.gridRows
    14→   * @param {object}      [config.aiEngine] - AIEngine instance (optional)
    15→   */
    16→  constructor(config = {}) {
    17→    this.walkable  = config.walkable  || [];
    18→    this.gridCols  = config.gridCols  || 19;
    19→    this.gridRows  = config.gridRows  || 13;
    20→    this.aiEngine  = config.aiEngine  || null;
    21→
    22→    this.characters = [];
    23→
    24→    // Object state machine engine — pre-loaded with Japanese Home objects
    25→    this.objectEngine = new ObjectEngine();
    26→    this.objectEngine.addObjects(OBJECT_DEFS);
    27→
    28→    // Events queued for scene to consume (emoji floats, etc.)
    29→    this.pendingEvents = [];
    30→
    31→    // Sim clock — starts at 08:00 AM game-time
    32→    this.simTimeMs = 8 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
    33→    // 1 real second = 60 sim seconds  (1 real min = 1 sim hour)
    34→    this.simSpeed  = 60;
    35→
    36→    // Cache walkable tiles list (built lazily)
    37→    this._walkableTiles = null;
    38→  }
    39→
    40→  addCharacter(char) {
    41→    this.characters.push(char);
    42→  }
    43→
    44→  // ── Main update loop ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    45→
    46→  update(deltaMs) {
    47→    // Advance sim clock
    48→    this.simTimeMs += deltaMs * this.simSpeed;
    49→
    50→    // Optional AI decisions — pass live object list so AI sees current states
    51→    if (this.aiEngine) {
    52→      this.aiEngine.update(deltaMs, this.characters, this.objectEngine.getAll(), {
    53→        timeString: this.getSimTimeString(),
    54→        findAdjacentWalkable: this._findAdjacentWalkable.bind(this),
    55→        pushEvent: (ev) => this.pendingEvents.push(ev),
    56→      });
    57→    }
    58→
    59→    // Tick object state machines; collect auto-transition events
    60→    const objEvents = this.objectEngine.tick(deltaMs);
    61→    for (const ev of objEvents) {
    62→      if (ev.emoji) this.pendingEvents.push(ev);
    63→    }
    64→
    65→    for (const char of this.characters) {
    66→      // Save pre-update state to detect interaction-end transitions
    67→      const prevAction         = char.action;
    68→      const prevInteractTarget = char.interactTarget;
    69→
    70→      // Handle arrival: character reached target object tile
    71→      if (char.action === 'idle' && char.targetObjectId) {
    72→        this._handleObjectArrival(char);
    73→      }
    74→
    75→      // Handle arrival: character reached talk target
    76→      if (char.action === 'idle' && char.pendingTalkTarget) {
    77→        this._handleTalkArrival(char);
    78→      }
    79→
    80→      // Mid-walk: periodically re-route toward a moving talk target
    81→      if (char.action === 'walking' && char.pendingTalkTarget) {
    82→        char._talkRetargetTimer -= deltaMs;
    83→        if (char._talkRetargetTimer <= 0) {
    84→          char._talkRetargetTimer = 2000; // re-check every 2 s
    85→          this._updateTalkRoute(char);
    86→        }
    87→      }
    88→
    89→      // Trigger random wander (or object visit) when idle and timer expired
    90→      if (char.action === 'idle' && char.wanderTimer <= 0) {
    91→        this._doWander(char);
    92→      }
    93→
    94→      // Tick speech timer — fire a random line when it expires
    95→      if (char.dialogue.length > 0 && char.pendingSpeech === null) {
    96→        char.speechTimer -= deltaMs;
    97→        if (char.speechTimer <= 0) {
    98→          const idx = Math.floor(Math.random() * char.dialogue.length);
    99→          char.pendingSpeech = char.dialogue[idx];
   100→          char.speechTimer   = 20000 + Math.random() * 20000; // reset 20–40 s
   101→        }
   102→      }
   103→
   104→      // Per-character update (movement, animations, sprite sync)
   105→      char.update(deltaMs);
   106→
   107→      // Detect interaction end: release slot so other characters can use the object
   108→      if (prevAction === 'interacting' && char.action !== 'interacting' && prevInteractTarget) {
   109→        this.objectEngine.release(prevInteractTarget, char.name);
   110→      }
   111→    }
   112→  }
   113→
   114→  // ── Object interaction ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   115→
   116→  /**
   117→   * Called when a character arrives at an object's adjacent tile.
   118→   * Fires the 'use' transition and puts the character into 'interacting' state.
   119→   * If the object has no valid transition, finds an alternative instead of idling.
   120→   */
   121→  _handleObjectArrival(char) {
   122→    const objectId = char.targetObjectId;
   123→    const action   = char.pendingAction || 'use';
   124→
   125→    // Clear targeting immediately so we don't re-fire on the next idle frame.
   126→    // _fallbackToAlternativeObject may set a new targetObjectId if it finds one.
   127→    char.targetObjectId = null;
   128→    char.pendingAction  = null;
   129→
   130→    const event = this.objectEngine.interact(objectId, action);
   131→
   132→    if (event) {
   133→      // Convert reservation → active occupancy
   134→      this.objectEngine.arrive(objectId, char.name);
   135→
   136→      const obj = this.objectEngine.getById(objectId);
   137→
   138→      // Hold the character for the full auto_next duration if the new state has one;
   139→      // otherwise fall back to the object's generic interactMs.
   140→      let holdMs = obj ? obj.interactMs : 8000;
   141→      if (obj && event.state) {
   142→        const stateDef = obj.states[event.state];
   143→        if (stateDef?.auto_next?.after) {
   144→          holdMs = stateDef.auto_next.after * 1000;
   145→        }
   146→      }
   147→
   148→      char.startInteraction(objectId, holdMs);
   149→
   150→      if (event.speech) char.pendingSpeech = event.speech;
   151→      if (event.emoji)  this.pendingEvents.push(event);
   152→    } else {
   153→      // No valid transition (object changed state mid-walk) — release the
   154→      // reservation and try to find an alternative object.
   155→      this.objectEngine.release(objectId, char.name);
   156→      this._fallbackToAlternativeObject(char, objectId);
   157→    }
   158→  }
   159→
   160→  // ── Talk handshake ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   161→
   162→  /**
   163→   * Called when a character arrives at the tile adjacent to their talk target.
   164→   * Checks proximity and re-evaluates B's availability before starting conversation.
   165→   */
   166→  _handleTalkArrival(char) {
   167→    const target = char.pendingTalkTarget;
   168→    char.pendingTalkTarget = null;
   169→
   170→    // Proximity check: target may have moved significantly during the walk.
   171→    const dx   = Math.round(target.tx) - Math.round(char.tx);
   172→    const dy   = Math.round(target.ty) - Math.round(char.ty);
   173→    const dist = Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy);
   174→
   175→    if (dist > 3) {
   176→      // Target has drifted — try to follow if not too far
   177→      if (dist <= 10) {
   178→        const adjTile = this._findAdjacentWalkable(Math.round(target.tx), Math.round(target.ty));
   179→        if (adjTile && char.moveTo(adjTile.tx, adjTile.ty)) {
   180→          // Re-attach pending talk so we retry on next arrival
   181→          char.pendingTalkTarget   = target;
   182→          char._talkRetargetTimer  = 2000;
   183→          return;
   184→        }
   185→      }
   186→      // Too far or unreachable — abort
   187→      this.pendingEvents.push({
   188→        type:      'fallback',
   189→        charLabel: char.label,
   190→        reason:    'talk_target_moved',
   191→        fromLabel: target.label,
   192→        toLabel:   null,
   193→      });
   194→      char.pendingTalkDialogue = null;
   195→      char.pendingTalkResponse = null;
   196→      char.wanderTimer = 3000 + Math.random() * 5000;
   197→      return;
   198→    }
   199→
   200→    // Re-check availability: accept if idle or walking, reject if busy
   201→    const canTalk = target.action === 'idle' || target.action === 'walking';
   202→
   203→    if (!canTalk) {
   204→      this.pendingEvents.push({
   205→        type:           'talk_rejected',
   206→        initiatorLabel: char.label,
   207→        targetLabel:    target.label,
   208→      });
   209→      char.wanderTimer = 3000 + Math.random() * 5000;
   210→      return;
   211→    }
   212→
   213→    this._startConversation(char, target);
   214→  }
   215→
   216→  /**
   217→   * Configurable conversation duration range (ms).
   218→   * Defaults to 10–15 s; override via constructor config.
   219→   */
   220→  get _talkDurationMs() {
   221→    return 10_000 + Math.random() * 5_000;
   222→  }
   223→
   224→  /**
   225→   * Synchronise charA and charB into a shared 'talking' state.
   226→   * Both face each other, AI timers are paused (via action check in AIEngine),
   227→   * and conversation ends naturally when the timer expires.
   228→   */
   229→  _startConversation(charA, charB) {
   230→    const duration = this._talkDurationMs;
   231→
   232→    // Face each other
   233→    const dx = Math.round(charB.tx) - Math.round(charA.tx);
   234→    const dy = Math.round(charB.ty) - Math.round(charA.ty);
   235→    if (Math.abs(dx) >= Math.abs(dy)) {
   236→      charA.facing = dx >= 0 ? 'right' : 'left';
   237→      charB.facing = dx >= 0 ? 'left'  : 'right';
   238→    } else {
   239→      charA.facing = dy >= 0 ? 'down' : 'up';
   240→      charB.facing = dy >= 0 ? 'up'   : 'down';
   241→    }
   242→
   243→    // Transfer queued dialogue to speech bubbles
   244→    if (charA.pendingTalkDialogue) {
   245→      charA.pendingSpeech          = charA.pendingTalkDialogue;
   246→      charA.pendingTalkDialogue    = null;
   247→    }
   248→    if (charA.pendingTalkResponse) {
   249→      charB.pendingSpeech          = charA.pendingTalkResponse;
   250→      charA.pendingTalkResponse    = null;
   251→    }
   252→
   253→    charA.startTalk(charB, duration);
   254→    charB.startTalk(charA, duration);
   255→
   256→    this.pendingEvents.push({
   257→      type:           'conversation_start',
   258→      initiatorLabel: charA.label,
   259→      targetLabel:    charB.label,
   260→    });
   261→  }
   262→
   263→  // ── Wander ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   264→
   265→  _doWander(char) {
   266→    // 30% chance: walk to a random interactive object instead of wandering freely
   267→    if (Math.random() < 0.3) {
   268→      const objects = this.objectEngine.getAll();
   269→      if (objects.length > 0) {
   270→        // Shuffle and try each until one has an available slot and a reachable adjacent tile
   271→        const shuffled = objects.slice().sort(() => Math.random() - 0.5);
   272→        for (const obj of shuffled) {
   273→          if (obj.isFull()) continue; // skip objects at capacity
   274→          // Only target objects whose current state accepts a 'use' interaction
   275→          const stateDef = obj.states[obj.state];
   276→          if (!stateDef?.transitions?.use) continue;
   277→          const tile = this._findAdjacentWalkable(obj.tx, obj.ty);
   278→          if (tile && char.moveTo(tile.tx, tile.ty)) {
   279→            obj.reserve(char.name); // claim a slot before walking
   280→            char.targetObjectId = obj.id;
   281→            char.pendingAction  = 'use';
   282→            return;
   283→          }
   284→        }
   285→        // All objects full/non-interactable/unreachable — fall through to random wander
   286→      }
   287→    }
   288→
   289→    // Random walkable tile
   290→    const tiles = this._getWalkableTiles();
   291→    if (tiles.length === 0) {
   292→      char.wanderTimer = 2000;
   293→      return;
   294→    }
   295→
   296→    const cx = Math.round(char.tx);
   297→    const cy = Math.round(char.ty);
   298→
   299→    let moved = false;
   300→    for (let attempt = 0; attempt < 15; attempt++) {
   301→      const tile = tiles[Math.floor(Math.random() * tiles.length)];
   302→      if (tile.tx === cx && tile.ty === cy) continue;
   303→      moved = char.moveTo(tile.tx, tile.ty);
   304→      if (moved) break;
   305→    }
   306→
   307→    if (!moved) {
   308→      char.wanderTimer = 2000;
   309→    }
   310→  }
   311→
   312→  // ── Fallback helpers ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   313→
   314→  /**
   315→   * Find the closest available object that `char` can interact with right now,
   316→   * excluding the object with `excludeId`.
   317→   * @returns {ObjectInstance|null}
   318→   */
   319→  _findAlternativeObject(char, excludeId) {
   320→    const objects = this.objectEngine.getAll();
   321→    let best     = null;
   322→    let bestDist = Infinity;
   323→
   324→    for (const obj of objects) {
   325→      if (obj.id === excludeId) continue;
   326→      if (obj.isFull()) continue;
   327→      // Require a usable state right now
   328→      const stateDef = obj.states[obj.state];
   329→      if (!stateDef?.transitions?.use) continue;
   330→      // Require a reachable adjacent tile
   331→      if (!this._findAdjacentWalkable(obj.tx, obj.ty)) continue;
   332→
   333→      const dx   = obj.tx - Math.round(char.tx);
   334→      const dy   = obj.ty - Math.round(char.ty);
   335→      const dist = dx * dx + dy * dy;
   336→      if (dist < bestDist) { bestDist = dist; best = obj; }
   337→    }
   338→
   339→    return best;
   340→  }
   341→
   342→  /**
   343→   * Called when a character's object interaction fails on arrival.
   344→   * Tries to redirect to the nearest available alternative; emits a 'fallback' event.
   345→   */
   346→  _fallbackToAlternativeObject(char, fromId) {
   347→    const fromObj     = this.objectEngine.getById(fromId);
   348→    const alternative = this._findAlternativeObject(char, fromId);
   349→
   350→    if (alternative) {
   351→      const adjTile = this._findAdjacentWalkable(alternative.tx, alternative.ty);
   352→      if (adjTile && char.moveTo(adjTile.tx, adjTile.ty)) {
   353→        alternative.reserve(char.name);
   354→        char.targetObjectId = alternative.id;
   355→        char.pendingAction  = 'use';
   356→
   357→        this.pendingEvents.push({
   358→          type:      'fallback',
   359→          charLabel: char.label,
   360→          reason:    'object_unavailable',
   361→          fromLabel: fromObj?.name ?? fromId,
   362→          toLabel:   alternative.name,
   363→        });
   364→        return;
   365→      }
   366→    }
   367→
   368→    // No usable alternative — idle
   369→    char.wanderTimer = 3000 + Math.random() * 5000;
   370→    this.pendingEvents.push({
   371→      type:      'fallback',
   372→      charLabel: char.label,
   373→      reason:    'object_unavailable',
   374→      fromLabel: fromObj?.name ?? fromId,
   375→      toLabel:   null,
   376→    });
   377→  }
   378→
   379→  /**
   380→   * Called periodically while a character is walking toward a talk target.
   381→   * Re-routes the character if the target has moved, or aborts if too far.
   382→   */
   383→  _updateTalkRoute(char) {
   384→    const target = char.pendingTalkTarget;
   385→    if (!target) return;
   386→
   387→    const dx   = Math.round(target.tx) - Math.round(char.tx);
   388→    const dy   = Math.round(target.ty) - Math.round(char.ty);
   389→    const dist = Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy);
   390→
   391→    // If target has wandered more than 10 tiles away, give up
   392→    if (dist > 10) {
   393→      char.pendingTalkTarget   = null;
   394→      char.pendingTalkDialogue = null;
   395→      char.pendingTalkResponse = null;
   396→      char.path                = [];
   397→      char.action              = 'idle';
   398→      char.wanderTimer         = 3000 + Math.random() * 5000;
   399→
   400→      this.pendingEvents.push({
   401→        type:      'fallback',
   402→        charLabel: char.label,
   403→        reason:    'talk_target_moved',
   404→        fromLabel: target.label,
   405→        toLabel:   null,
   406→      });
   407→      return;
   408→    }
   409→
   410→    // Re-route only if the path end has drifted more than 1 tile from target
   411→    const pathEnd = char.path[char.path.length - 1];
   412→    if (pathEnd) {
   413→      const edx = pathEnd.tx - Math.round(target.tx);
   414→      const edy = pathEnd.ty - Math.round(target.ty);
   415→      if (Math.sqrt(edx * edx + edy * edy) > 1) {
   416→        const adjTile = this._findAdjacentWalkable(Math.round(target.tx), Math.round(target.ty));
   417→        if (adjTile) char.moveTo(adjTile.tx, adjTile.ty);
   418→      }
   419→    }
   420→  }
   421→
   422→  /**
   423→   * Return the first walkable tile cardinally adjacent to (tx, ty), or null.
   424→   */
   425→  _findAdjacentWalkable(tx, ty) {
   426→    const dirs = [
   427→      { tx, ty: ty - 1 },
   428→      { tx, ty: ty + 1 },
   429→      { tx: tx - 1, ty },
   430→      { tx: tx + 1, ty },
   431→    ];
   432→    for (const d of dirs) {
   433→      if (d.tx >= 0 && d.tx < this.gridCols && d.ty >= 0 && d.ty < this.gridRows) {
   434→        if (this.walkable[d.ty]?.[d.tx]) return d;
   435→      }
   436→    }
   437→    return null;
   438→  }
   439→
   440→  _getWalkableTiles() {
   441→    if (this._walkableTiles) return this._walkableTiles;
   442→    const tiles = [];
   443→    for (let row = 0; row < this.gridRows; row++) {
   444→      for (let col = 0; col < this.gridCols; col++) {
   445→        if (this.walkable[row]?.[col]) tiles.push({ tx: col, ty: row });
   446→      }
   447→    }
   448→    this._walkableTiles = tiles;
   449→    return tiles;
   450→  }
   451→
   452→  // ── Sim clock ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   453→
   454→  getSimTimeString() {
   455→    const totalSec = Math.floor(this.simTimeMs / 1000);
   456→    const hours    = Math.floor(totalSec / 3600) % 24;
   457→    const minutes  = Math.floor((totalSec % 3600) / 60);
   458→    const ampm     = hours >= 12 ? 'PM' : 'AM';
   459→    const h        = hours % 12 || 12;
   460→    return `${h}:${String(minutes).padStart(2, '0')} ${ampm}`;
   461→  }
   462→}
   463→

     1→/**
     2→ * Character.js — tile-based character with A* pathfinding and state machine.
     3→ * Pure JS, no Phaser dependency. Sprite/label references are set externally.
     4→ */
     5→
     6→const TILE_SIZE = 48;
     7→
     8→// ─── A* pathfinding ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
     9→
    10→function heuristic(ax, ay, bx, by) {
    11→  return Math.abs(ax - bx) + Math.abs(ay - by);
    12→}
    13→
    14→/**
    15→ * Find a path from (startX, startY) to (goalX, goalY) on a walkable grid.
    16→ * @param {boolean[][]} walkable  - walkable[row][col]
    17→ * @param {number} cols
    18→ * @param {number} rows
    19→ * @returns {Array<{tx,ty}>|null}  - list of steps NOT including start; null if no path
    20→ */
    21→function findPath(walkable, cols, rows, startX, startY, goalX, goalY) {
    22→  if (startX === goalX && startY === goalY) return [];
    23→  if (!walkable[startY]?.[startX] || !walkable[goalY]?.[goalX]) return null;
    24→
    25→  const key = (x, y) => x * 1000 + y;
    26→
    27→  const open = new Map();
    28→  const closed = new Set();
    29→
    30→  const startNode = { x: startX, y: startY, g: 0, h: heuristic(startX, startY, goalX, goalY), parent: null };
    31→  open.set(key(startX, startY), startNode);
    32→
    33→  while (open.size > 0) {
    34→    // Pick node with lowest f = g + h
    35→    let current = null;
    36→    for (const node of open.values()) {
    37→      if (!current || node.g + node.h < current.g + current.h) current = node;
    38→    }
    39→
    40→    if (current.x === goalX && current.y === goalY) {
    41→      // Reconstruct path
    42→      const path = [];
    43→      let node = current;
    44→      while (node.parent) {
    45→        path.unshift({ tx: node.x, ty: node.y });
    46→        node = node.parent;
    47→      }
    48→      return path;
    49→    }
    50→
    51→    open.delete(key(current.x, current.y));
    52→    closed.add(key(current.x, current.y));
    53→
    54→    const neighbors = [
    55→      { x: current.x + 1, y: current.y },
    56→      { x: current.x - 1, y: current.y },
    57→      { x: current.x,     y: current.y + 1 },
    58→      { x: current.x,     y: current.y - 1 },
    59→    ];
    60→
    61→    for (const n of neighbors) {
    62→      if (n.x < 0 || n.x >= cols || n.y < 0 || n.y >= rows) continue;
    63→      if (!walkable[n.y]?.[n.x]) continue;
    64→      if (closed.has(key(n.x, n.y))) continue;
    65→
    66→      const g = current.g + 1;
    67→      const existing = open.get(key(n.x, n.y));
    68→      if (existing) {
    69→        if (g < existing.g) {
    70→          existing.g = g;
    71→          existing.parent = current;
    72→        }
    73→      } else {
    74→        open.set(key(n.x, n.y), {
    75→          x: n.x, y: n.y,
    76→          g, h: heuristic(n.x, n.y, goalX, goalY),
    77→          parent: current,
    78→        });
    79→      }
    80→    }
    81→  }
    82→
    83→  return null; // no path
    84→}
    85→
    86→// ─── Character ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    87→
    88→export class Character {
    89→  /**
    90→   * @param {object} config
    91→   * @param {string}   config.name        - sprite key prefix (e.g. 'Amelia')
    92→   * @param {string}   config.label       - display name (e.g. 'Maple')
    93→   * @param {number}   config.tx          - starting tile X
    94→   * @param {number}   config.ty          - starting tile Y
    95→   * @param {boolean[][]} config.walkable - walkable grid [row][col]
    96→   * @param {number}   config.gridCols
    97→   * @param {number}   config.gridRows
    98→   * @param {object}   [config.sprite]    - Phaser sprite (set after construction)
    99→   * @param {object}   [config.nameLabel] - Phaser Text object
   100→   * @param {number}   [config.moveSpeed] - tiles per second (default 2)
   101→   */
   102→  constructor(config) {
   103→    this.name      = config.name;
   104→    this.label     = config.label;
   105→    this.sprite    = config.sprite    || null;
   106→    this.nameLabel = config.nameLabel || null;
   107→
   108→    this.tx     = config.tx;
   109→    this.ty     = config.ty;
   110→    this.prevTx = config.tx;
   111→    this.prevTy = config.ty;
   112→
   113→    this.path        = [];
   114→    this.moveProgress = 0;
   115→    this.moveSpeed   = config.moveSpeed || 2; // tiles/sec
   116→
   117→    // State: 'idle' | 'walking' | 'interacting' | 'talking'
   118→    this.action = 'idle';
   119→    this.facing = 'down';
   120→
   121→    // Wander: timer counts DOWN; engine starts wander when <= 0
   122→    this.wanderTimer = 3000 + Math.random() * 5000; // 3–8 s
   123→
   124→    // Interaction
   125→    this.interactTimer    = 0;
   126→    this.interactTimerMax = 0; // initial duration; used by UI for progress bar
   127→    this.interactTarget   = null;
   128→
   129→    // Personality stats (0–100)
   130→    this.mood   = 100;
   131→    this.energy = 100;
   132→
   133→    // Optional dialogue driven by AI
   134→    this.currentDialogue = null;
   135→    this.dialogueTimer   = 0;
   136→
   137→    // Preset dialogue lines (used for random speech bubbles)
   138→    this.dialogue     = config.dialogue || [];
   139→    // Counts down; when it hits 0 Engine sets pendingSpeech
   140→    this.speechTimer  = 20000 + Math.random() * 20000; // 20–40 s
   141→    // Scene reads this each frame and shows a bubble, then clears it
   142→    this.pendingSpeech = null;
   143→
   144→    this.walkable  = config.walkable;
   145→    this.gridCols  = config.gridCols;
   146→    this.gridRows  = config.gridRows;
   147→
   148→    // Object interaction targeting — set by engine, cleared on arrival
   149→    this.targetObjectId = null;
   150→    this.pendingAction  = null;
   151→
   152→    // Fallback/re-routing: counts down; engine updates talk route when <= 0
   153→    this._talkRetargetTimer = 0;
   154→
   155→    // Talk targeting — set by AIEngine when walking to meet another character
   156→    this.pendingTalkTarget   = null;  // Character ref awaiting arrival
   157→    this.pendingTalkDialogue = null;  // What A will say when conversation starts
   158→    this.pendingTalkResponse = null;  // What B will say when conversation starts
   159→
   160→    // Active conversation state
   161→    this.talkTimer    = 0;
   162→    this.talkTimerMax = 0;
   163→    this.talkTarget   = null;  // Character ref of current conversation partner
   164→  }
   165→
   166→  // ── Computed pixel position (Phaser setOrigin(0.5, 1) — feet at py) ─────────
   167→
   168→  get px() {
   169→    if (this.path.length === 0) {
   170→      return this.tx * TILE_SIZE + TILE_SIZE / 2;
   171→    }
   172→    const next = this.path[0];
   173→    return (this.prevTx + (next.tx - this.prevTx) * this.moveProgress) * TILE_SIZE + TILE_SIZE / 2;
   174→  }
   175→
   176→  get py() {
   177→    if (this.path.length === 0) {
   178→      return (this.ty + 1) * TILE_SIZE;
   179→    }
   180→    const next = this.path[0];
   181→    return (this.prevTy + (next.ty - this.prevTy) * this.moveProgress + 1) * TILE_SIZE;
   182→  }
   183→
   184→  // ── Movement ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   185→
   186→  moveTo(goalTx, goalTy) {
   187→    const sx = Math.round(this.tx);
   188→    const sy = Math.round(this.ty);
   189→    const path = findPath(this.walkable, this.gridCols, this.gridRows, sx, sy, goalTx, goalTy);
   190→
   191→    if (path && path.length > 0) {
   192→      this.path         = path;
   193→      this.prevTx       = sx;
   194→      this.prevTy       = sy;
   195→      this.moveProgress = 0;
   196→      this.action       = 'walking';
   197→
   198→      // Set initial facing from first step
   199→      this._updateFacingFromNextTile();
   200→      this._playWalkAnim();
   201→      return true;
   202→    }
   203→    return false;
   204→  }
   205→
   206→  /** Convenience wrapper — start interaction with a named object. */
   207→  startInteraction(objectId, durationMs) {
   208→    this.startInteract(objectId, durationMs);
   209→  }
   210→
   211→  startInteract(target, durationMs) {
   212→    this.action           = 'interacting';
   213→    this.interactTarget   = target;
   214→    this.interactTimer    = durationMs;
   215→    this.interactTimerMax = durationMs;
   216→    if (this.sprite) {
   217→      this.sprite.play(`${this.name}_idle_anim`, true);
   218→    }
   219→  }
   220→
   221→  /** Enter a shared talking state with `partner` for `durationMs` milliseconds. */
   222→  startTalk(partner, durationMs) {
   223→    // Stop any current movement
   224→    this.path        = [];
   225→    this.moveProgress = 0;
   226→
   227→    this.action       = 'talking';
   228→    this.talkTarget   = partner;
   229→    this.talkTimer    = durationMs;
   230→    this.talkTimerMax = durationMs;
   231→
   232→    // Clear any pending object interaction targeting
   233→    this.targetObjectId      = null;
   234→    this.pendingAction       = null;
   235→    // Clear any pending talk targeting (e.g. B was also walking to someone)
   236→    this.pendingTalkTarget   = null;
   237→    this.pendingTalkDialogue = null;
   238→    this.pendingTalkResponse = null;
   239→
   240→    if (this.sprite) {
   241→      this.sprite.play(`${this.name}_idle_anim`, true);
   242→    }
   243→  }
   244→
   245→  // ── Per-frame update ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   246→
   247→  update(deltaMs) {
   248→    if (this.action === 'walking' && this.path.length > 0) {
   249→      const tileDurationMs = 1000 / this.moveSpeed;
   250→      this.moveProgress += deltaMs / tileDurationMs;
   251→
   252→      // Update facing toward next tile in path
   253→      this._updateFacingFromNextTile();
   254→
   255→      // Advance tiles
   256→      while (this.moveProgress >= 1 && this.path.length > 0) {
   257→        this.moveProgress -= 1;
   258→        const arrived = this.path.shift();
   259→        this.prevTx = arrived.tx;
   260→        this.prevTy = arrived.ty;
   261→        this.tx     = arrived.tx;
   262→        this.ty     = arrived.ty;
   263→      }
   264→
   265→      if (this.path.length === 0) {
   266→        this.moveProgress = 0;
   267→        this.action       = 'idle';
   268→        this.wanderTimer  = 3000 + Math.random() * 5000;
   269→        this._playAnim('idle');
   270→      } else {
   271→        this._playWalkAnim();
   272→      }
   273→    } else if (this.action === 'idle') {
   274→      this.wanderTimer -= deltaMs;
   275→    } else if (this.action === 'interacting') {
   276→      this.interactTimer -= deltaMs;
   277→      if (this.interactTimer <= 0) {
   278→        this.action        = 'idle';
   279→        this.interactTarget = null;
   280→        this.wanderTimer   = 3000 + Math.random() * 5000;
   281→        this._playAnim('idle');
   282→      }
   283→    } else if (this.action === 'talking') {
   284→      this.talkTimer -= deltaMs;
   285→      if (this.talkTimer <= 0) {
   286→        this.action      = 'idle';
   287→        this.talkTarget  = null;
   288→        this.wanderTimer = 3000 + Math.random() * 5000;
   289→        this._playAnim('idle');
   290→      }
   291→    }
   292→
   293→    // Tick dialogue
   294→    if (this.dialogueTimer > 0) {
   295→      this.dialogueTimer -= deltaMs;
   296→      if (this.dialogueTimer <= 0) this.currentDialogue = null;
   297→    }
   298→
   299→    // Sync Phaser sprite
   300→    if (this.sprite) {
   301→      this.sprite.x = this.px;
   302→      this.sprite.y = this.py;
   303→    }
   304→
   305→    if (this.nameLabel && this.sprite) {
   306→      this.nameLabel.setPosition(this.sprite.x, this.sprite.y - 100);
   307→    }
   308→  }
   309→
   310→  // ── Perception ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   311→
   312→  /** Returns objects within `radius` tiles. */
   313→  getPerceivedObjects(objects, radius = 4) {
   314→    return objects.filter(obj => {
   315→      const dx = obj.tx - this.tx;
   316→      const dy = obj.ty - this.ty;
   317→      return Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy) <= radius;
   318→    });
   319→  }
   320→
   321→  // ── Animation helpers ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   322→
   323→  _updateFacingFromNextTile() {
   324→    if (this.path.length === 0) return;
   325→    const next = this.path[0];
   326→    const dx   = next.tx - this.tx;
   327→    const dy   = next.ty - this.ty;
   328→    if (Math.abs(dx) >= Math.abs(dy)) {
   329→      this.facing = dx >= 0 ? 'right' : 'left';
   330→    } else {
   331→      this.facing = dy > 0 ? 'down' : 'up';
   332→    }
   333→  }
   334→
   335→  _playAnim(type) {
   336→    if (!this.sprite) return;
   337→    const key = type === 'idle'
   338→      ? `${this.name}_idle_anim`
   339→      : `${this.name}_walk_${this.facing}`;
   340→    if (this.sprite.anims.currentAnim?.key !== key) {
   341→      this.sprite.play(key, true);
   342→    }
   343→    this.sprite.flipX = (type === 'walk' && this.facing === 'left');
   344→  }
   345→
   346→  _playWalkAnim() {
   347→    this._playAnim('walk');
   348→  }
   349→}
   350→

   215→
   216→// ── ObjectInstance ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   217→
   218→class ObjectInstance {
   219→  constructor(def) {
   220→    this.id        = def.id;
   221→    this.name      = def.name;
   222→    this.label     = def.name;           // compat for AIEngine
   223→    this.position  = def.position;
   224→    this.tx        = def.position.tx;    // compat for AIEngine distance checks
   225→    this.ty        = def.position.ty;
   226→    this.states    = def.states;
   227→    this.state     = def.state || 'idle';
   228→    this.interactMs = def.interactMs || 8000;
   229→    this.autoTimer = 0;
   230→    this._resetAutoTimer();
   231→
   232→    // Slot system
   233→    this.capacity      = def.capacity ?? 1;
   234→    this._reservations = new Set(); // charNames walking toward this object
   235→    this._occupants    = new Set(); // charNames actively interacting
   236→  }
   237→
   238→  /** True if no more slots are available (reserved + occupied >= capacity). */
   239→  isFull() {
   240→    return this._reservations.size + this._occupants.size >= this.capacity;
   241→  }
   242→
   243→  /**
   244→   * Reserve a slot for charName before they start walking.
   245→   * Returns true if the reservation succeeded, false if the object is full.
   246→   */
   247→  reserve(charName) {
   248→    if (this.isFull()) return false;
   249→    this._reservations.add(charName);
   250→    return true;
   251→  }
   252→
   253→  /**
   254→   * Called when charName arrives at the object.
   255→   * Converts the reservation to an active occupancy.
   256→   */
   257→  arrive(charName) {
   258→    this._reservations.delete(charName);
   259→    this._occupants.add(charName);
   260→  }
   261→
   262→  /**
   263→   * Release a slot when the character finishes interacting or abandons the walk.
   264→   */
   265→  release(charName) {
   266→    this._reservations.delete(charName);
   267→    this._occupants.delete(charName);
   268→  }
   269→
   270→  /** Returns the names of characters who have reserved a slot (walking toward this object). */
   271→  getReservations() { return Array.from(this._reservations); }
   272→
   273→  /** Returns the names of characters who are actively occupying a slot. */
   274→  getOccupants() { return Array.from(this._occupants); }
   275→
   276→  /** Clear all reservations and occupancies (used on sim reset). */
   277→  clearSlots() {
   278→    this._reservations.clear();
   279→    this._occupants.clear();
   280→  }
   281→
   282→  /**
   283→   * Returns current slot occupancy info.
   284→   * @returns {{ capacity, reserved, occupied, available }}
   285→   */
   286→  getSlotInfo() {
   287→    return {
   288→      capacity:  this.capacity,
   289→      reserved:  this._reservations.size,
   290→      occupied:  this._occupants.size,
   291→      available: this.capacity - this._reservations.size - this._occupants.size,
   292→    };
   293→  }
   294→
   295→  _resetAutoTimer() {
   296→    const s = this.states[this.state];
   297→    this.autoTimer = s?.auto_next ? s.auto_next.after * 1000 : 0;
   298→  }
   299→
   300→  /**
   301→   * Trigger an interaction action (e.g. 'use').
   302→   * @returns {{ objectId, state, speech, emoji }|null}
   303→   */
   304→  interact(action = 'use') {
   305→    const s  = this.states[this.state];
   306→    const tr = s?.transitions?.[action];
   307→    if (!tr) return null;
   308→
   309→    this.state = tr.next;
   310→    this._resetAutoTimer();
   311→
   312→    const ns = this.states[this.state];
   313→    return {
   314→      objectId: this.id,
   315→      state:    this.state,
   316→      speech:   ns?.speech || null,
   317→      emoji:    ns?.emoji  || null,
   318→    };
   319→  }
   320→
   321→  /**
   322→   * Advance auto_next timers.
   323→   * @returns {{ objectId, state, emoji, auto: true }|null}
   324→   */
   325→  tick(deltaMs) {
   326→    if (this.autoTimer <= 0) return null;
   327→
   328→    this.autoTimer -= deltaMs;
   329→    if (this.autoTimer > 0) return null;
   330→
   331→    const s = this.states[this.state];
   332→    if (!s?.auto_next) return null;
   333→
   334→    this.state = s.auto_next.state;
   335→    this._resetAutoTimer();
   336→
   337→    const ns = this.states[this.state];
   338→    return {
   339→      objectId: this.id,
   340→      state:    this.state,
   341→      emoji:    ns?.emoji || null,
   342→      auto:     true,
   343→    };
   344→  }
   345→}
   346→
   347→// ── ObjectEngine ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   348→
   349→export class ObjectEngine {
   350→  constructor() {
   351→    this._map = new Map(); // id → ObjectInstance
   352→  }
   353→
   354→  addObjects(defs) {
   355→    for (const def of defs) {
   356→      this._map.set(def.id, new ObjectInstance(def));
   357→    }
   358→  }
   359→
   360→  /**
   361→   * Tick all object timers. Returns any events that fired this frame.
   362→   * @returns {Array<{ objectId, state, emoji, auto }>}
   363→   */
   364→  tick(deltaMs) {
   365→    const events = [];
   366→    for (const obj of this._map.values()) {
   367→      const ev = obj.tick(deltaMs);
   368→      if (ev) events.push(ev);
   369→    }
   370→    return events;
   371→  }
   372→
   373→  /**
   374→   * Trigger an action on an object (e.g. 'use').
   375→   * @returns {{ objectId, state, speech, emoji }|null}

ASSISTANTMESSAGE #18
Now I understand the full picture. Let me analyze the root cause of the stale slot issue: **Current flow in Engine.js:** ```javascript for (const char of this.characters) { // Save pre-update state to detect interaction-end transitions const prevAction = char.action; const prevInteractTarget = char.interactTarget; // Handle arrival: character reached target object tile if (char.action === 'idle' && char.targetObjectId) { this._handleObjectArrival(char); } // ... other handlers ... // Per-character update (movement, animations, sprite sync) ``` I'm updating the character state and then checking if they've finished interacting so I can release the slot. The problem is with how the object state machine handles its `auto_next` timers—when a character starts interacting with the stove, the state transitions from `idle` to `cooking` with an automatic timer, but... Detecting interaction end... ``` 30s to 'done') 2. The character's `interactTimer` is set to either `obj.interactMs` (8000ms) or `stateDef.auto_next.after * 1000` (30000ms for cooking) Looking at `_handleObjectArrival`: ```javascript let holdMs = obj ? obj.interactMs : 8000; if (obj && event.state) { const stateDef = obj.states[event.state]; if (stateDef?.auto_next?.after) { holdMs = stateDef.auto_next.after * 1000; } } char.startInteraction(objectId, holdMs); ``` So for the stove: `cooking` state has `auto_next: { state: 'done', after: 30 }`, so hold Ms = 30000ms. The `done` state then has its own `auto_next: { state: 'idle', after: 60 }`, meaning after the cooking finishes, there's another 60-second wait before the object returns to idle. When the character's interaction timer expires at 30 seconds, the character clears its interaction state and target, which triggers the engine to release the object. The release logic checks if the character was previously interacting and clears that reference. ``` javascript const prevAction = char.action; const prevInteractTarget = char.interactTarget; ``` These values are captured before the character updates, so even though `char.update()` clears the interaction target, the engine still has the previous reference needed to properly release the object. Now I'm tracing through the actual sequence: the object engine ticks first, and if the stove's auto_next timer fires (transitioning from cooking to done), that happens before the character loop even runs. So the character's interactTimer might still be counting down while the object has already moved to a different state—that could be why the release isn't firing. But the issue description says only Reset clears stale slots, which means release() isn't being called at all. Let me check if there's a mismatch in the identifiers being used—the character stores the objectId in interactTarget, and both arrive() and release() use char.name, so those should align. I need to verify what's actually being passed to startInteract and whether the target identifier is consistent throughout. I'm realizing the state capture at the start of the loop protects against this—`prevAction` is set to `idle` before `_handleObjectArrival` changes it to `interacting`, so the detection logic won't fire until the next frame when the state transition is actually visible. Now I'm considering another edge case: what if `startTalk` is called while a character is already interacting? The method clears `targetObjectId` and `pendingAction`, but leaves `interactTarget` still pointing to the object, creating a mismatch where the action changes to `talking` but the target reference lingers. Actually, `startTalk` only gets called from `_startConversation` when the character is idle with a pending talk target, so this shouldn't happen unless the AI engine is calling it directly. Let me check if AIEngine can trigger talk while a character is mid-interaction. Wait, looking back at the issue's third possible cause about `_handleObjectArrival` clearing `targetObjectId` before `startInteraction` runs—that's the ordering problem I should focus on.      1→/**
     2→ * AIEngine.js — LLM-driven decision engine.
     3→ *
     4→ * When `endpoint` is null (default) the engine is disabled and characters
     5→ * fall back to random wander controlled by SimulationEngine.
     6→ *
     7→ * To enable, pass an endpoint URL and optionally an API key:
     8→ *   new AIEngine({ endpoint: 'https://api.anthropic.com/v1/messages', apiKey: '...' })
     9→ *
    10→ * The engine polls each character independently on a configurable interval.
    11→ * Responses are expected as JSON with this shape:
    12→ *   { "action": "move|interact|idle|talk",
    13→ *     "targetId": "object_id",               // for interact
    14→ *     "targetTile": { "tx": 5, "ty": 9 },    // for move
    15→ *     "targetCharacter": "character_name",   // for talk
    16→ *     "dialogue": "optional speech",
    17→ *     "targetDialogue": "response from target character", // for talk
    18→ *     "description": "what the character is doing" }
    19→ */
    20→
    21→export class AIEngine {
    22→  /**
    23→   * @param {object}  [config]
    24→   * @param {string}  [config.endpoint]            - full URL of LLM API endpoint
    25→   * @param {string}  [config.apiKey]              - bearer token / API key
    26→   * @param {string}  [config.model]               - model ID (for Anthropic-style APIs)
    27→   * @param {number}  [config.decisionIntervalMs]  - ms between decisions per char (default 30 000)
    28→   */
    29→  constructor(config = {}) {
    30→    this.endpoint           = config.endpoint           || null;
    31→    this.apiKey             = config.apiKey             || null;
    32→    this.model              = config.model              || 'claude-sonnet-4-6';
    33→    this.decisionIntervalMs = config.decisionIntervalMs || 30_000;
    34→    this.onDecision         = config.onDecision         || null;
    35→
    36→    this.enabled = !!this.endpoint;
    37→
    38→    // Per-character countdown timers  { name → ms until next decision }
    39→    this._timers = new Map();
    40→    // Prevent overlapping requests  { name → true }
    41→    this._pending = new Set();
    42→  }
    43→
    44→  // ── Called by SimulationEngine each frame ─────────────────────────────────
    45→
    46→  update(deltaMs, characters, objects, simState) {
    47→    if (!this.enabled) return;
    48→
    49→    for (const char of characters) {
    50→      let t = this._timers.get(char.name) ?? 0;
    51→      t -= deltaMs;
    52→
    53→      // Don't make decisions while character is held at an object or in conversation;
    54→      // let the timer keep ticking so the cooldown UI stays accurate.
    55→      if (t <= 0 && !this._pending.has(char.name) && char.action !== 'interacting' && char.action !== 'talking') {
    56→        this._timers.set(char.name, this.decisionIntervalMs);
    57→        this._requestDecision(char, characters, objects, simState);
    58→      } else {
    59→        this._timers.set(char.name, t);
    60→      }
    61→    }
    62→  }
    63→
    64→  // ── Internal ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    65→
    66→  async _requestDecision(character, characters, objects, simState) {
    67→    this._pending.add(character.name);
    68→
    69→    try {
    70→      const nearbyObjects = objects
    71→        .filter(obj => {
    72→          const dx = obj.tx - character.tx;
    73→          const dy = obj.ty - character.ty;
    74→          return Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy) <= 8;
    75→        })
    76→        .map(o => {
    77→          const slot = o.getSlotInfo();
    78→          // Resolve reserved/occupied character names → display labels for LLM context
    79→          const reservedBy = (o.getReservations?.() ?? [])
    80→            .map(n => characters.find(c => c.name === n)?.label ?? n);
    81→          const occupiedBy = (o.getOccupants?.() ?? [])
    82→            .map(n => characters.find(c => c.name === n)?.label ?? n);
    83→          return {
    84→            id:         o.id,
    85→            label:      o.label,
    86→            state:      o.state,
    87→            slots:      `${slot.available}/${slot.capacity} available`,
    88→            available:  slot.available > 0,
    89→            // Blackboard: show who is already heading here or using it
    90→            intendedBy: reservedBy,
    91→            usedBy:     occupiedBy,
    92→          };
    93→        });
    94→
    95→      const nearbyCharacters = characters
    96→        .filter(c => {
    97→          if (c.name === character.name) return false;
    98→          const dx = c.tx - character.tx;
    99→          const dy = c.ty - character.ty;
   100→          return Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy) <= 8;
   101→        })
   102→        .map(c => ({
   103→          label:   c.label,
   104→          tx:      Math.round(c.tx),
   105→          ty:      Math.round(c.ty),
   106→          action:  c.action,
   107→          canTalk: c.action === 'idle' || c.action === 'walking',
   108→        }));
   109→
   110→      const systemPrompt =
   111→        `You are ${character.label}, a character in a cosy Japanese home simulation. ` +
   112→        `Decide what to do next based on your mood (${character.mood}/100) and energy (${character.energy}/100). ` +
   113→        `Reply ONLY with valid JSON — no markdown fences, no extra text.`;
   114→
   115→      const userPrompt =
   116→        `Sim time: ${simState.timeString}. ` +
   117→        `You are at tile (${Math.round(character.tx)}, ${Math.round(character.ty)}). ` +
   118→        `Current action: ${character.action}. ` +
   119→        `Nearby objects: ${JSON.stringify(nearbyObjects)}. ` +
   120→        `Nearby characters: ${JSON.stringify(nearbyCharacters)}. ` +
   121→        `Choose one action:
` +
   122→        `  { "action": "move",     "targetTile": {"tx": N, "ty": N}, "dialogue": "...", "description": "..." }
` +
   123→        `  { "action": "interact", "targetId": "object_id",          "dialogue": "...", "description": "..." }
` +
   124→        `  { "action": "idle",                                        "dialogue": "...", "description": "..." }
` +
   125→        `  { "action": "talk",     "targetCharacter": "character_label", "dialogue": "what you say", "targetDialogue": "their response", "description": "..." }
` +
   126→        `IMPORTANT: Only choose "talk" if the target character has canTalk:true. Feel free to talk to any available character, not always the same one.`;
   127→
   128→      const headers = { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' };
   129→
   130→      // Build body — compatible with Anthropic Messages API shape by default;
   131→      // swap for OpenAI chat completions if needed by changing endpoint.
   132→      const body = JSON.stringify({
   133→        model: this.model,
   134→        max_tokens: 256,
   135→        system: systemPrompt,
   136→        messages: [{ role: 'user', content: userPrompt }],
   137→      });
   138→
   139→      const res = await fetch(this.endpoint, { method: 'POST', headers, body });
   140→
   141→      if (!res.ok) {
   142→        console.warn(`[AIEngine] ${character.name}: HTTP ${res.status}`);
   143→        return;
   144→      }
   145→
   146→      const data = await res.json();
   147→
   148→      // Extract text from Anthropic-style response; fall back to OpenAI style
   149→      let text = data?.content?.[0]?.text     // Anthropic
   150→              ?? data?.choices?.[0]?.message?.content // OpenAI
   151→              ?? null;
   152→
   153→      if (!text) {
   154→        console.warn(`[AIEngine] ${character.name}: unrecognised response shape`, data);
   155→        return;
   156→      }
   157→
   158→      const decision = JSON.parse(text);
   159→      this._applyDecision(character, decision, characters, objects, simState);
   160→    } catch (err) {
   161→      console.warn(`[AIEngine] ${character.name}:`, err);
   162→    } finally {
   163→      this._pending.delete(character.name);
   164→    }
   165→  }
   166→
   167→  _applyDecision(character, decision, characters, objects, simState) {
   168→    if (!decision?.action) return;
   169→
   170→    switch (decision.action) {
   171→      case 'move':
   172→        if (decision.targetTile) {
   173→          // Release any pending object reservation before moving freely
   174→          if (character.targetObjectId) {
   175→            const prevObj = objects.find(o => o.id === character.targetObjectId);
   176→            if (prevObj) {
   177→              prevObj.release(character.name);
   178→              if (simState?.pushEvent) {
   179→                simState.pushEvent({
   180→                  type:      'fallback',
   181→                  charLabel: character.label,
   182→                  reason:    'plan_changed',
   183→                  fromLabel: prevObj.label ?? prevObj.name,
   184→                  toLabel:   null,
   185→                });
   186→              }
   187→            }
   188→            character.targetObjectId = null;
   189→          }
   190→          character.moveTo(decision.targetTile.tx, decision.targetTile.ty);
   191→        }
   192→        break;
   193→
   194→      case 'interact': {
   195→        const obj = objects.find(o => o.id === decision.targetId);
   196→        if (obj) {
   197→          // If already heading to a different object, release that reservation first
   198→          let abandonedLabel = null;
   199→          if (character.targetObjectId && character.targetObjectId !== obj.id) {
   200→            const prevObj = objects.find(o => o.id === character.targetObjectId);
   201→            if (prevObj) {
   202→              prevObj.release(character.name);
   203→              abandonedLabel = prevObj.label ?? prevObj.name;
   204→            }
   205→            character.targetObjectId = null;
   206→          }
   207→
   208→          // Only commit if a slot is available and object is currently interactable
   209→          const stateDef = obj.states[obj.state];
   210→          if (!obj.isFull() && stateDef?.transitions?.use) {
   211→            // Walk to an adjacent walkable tile (same pattern as wander engine)
   212→            const adjTile = simState?.findAdjacentWalkable?.(obj.tx, obj.ty);
   213→            if (adjTile && character.moveTo(adjTile.tx, adjTile.ty)) {
   214→              if (obj.reserve(character.name)) { // claim slot; guard against any race
   215→                character.targetObjectId = obj.id;
   216→                character.pendingAction  = 'use';
   217→                if (abandonedLabel && simState?.pushEvent) {
   218→                  simState.pushEvent({
   219→                    type:      'fallback',
   220→                    charLabel: character.label,
   221→                    reason:    'plan_changed',
   222→                    fromLabel: abandonedLabel,
   223→                    toLabel:   obj.label ?? obj.name,
   224→                  });
   225→                }
   226→              }
   227→            }
   228→          } else if (abandonedLabel && simState?.pushEvent) {
   229→            // New target unavailable — character goes idle after abandoning previous
   230→            simState.pushEvent({
   231→              type:      'fallback',
   232→              charLabel: character.label,
   233→              reason:    'object_unavailable',
   234→              fromLabel: abandonedLabel,
   235→              toLabel:   null,
   236→            });
   237→          }
   238→        }
   239→        break;
   240→      }
   241→
   242→      case 'idle':
   243→        // Release any pending reservation, then stay put for one full decision interval
   244→        if (character.targetObjectId) {
   245→          const prevObj = objects.find(o => o.id === character.targetObjectId);
   246→          if (prevObj) {
   247→            prevObj.release(character.name);
   248→            if (simState?.pushEvent) {
   249→              simState.pushEvent({
   250→                type:      'fallback',
   251→                charLabel: character.label,
   252→                reason:    'plan_changed',
   253→                fromLabel: prevObj.label ?? prevObj.name,
   254→                toLabel:   null,
   255→              });
   256→            }
   257→          }
   258→          character.targetObjectId = null;
   259→        }
   260→        character.wanderTimer = this.decisionIntervalMs;
   261→        break;
   262→
   263→      case 'talk': {
   264→        const target = characters.find(c => c.label === decision.targetCharacter);
   265→        if (target) {
   266→          // Evaluate Phase: check if B can accept a conversation request.
   267→          // Accept if idle or walking; reject if interacting, talking, or otherwise busy.
   268→          const canAccept = target.action === 'idle' || target.action === 'walking';
   269→
   270→          if (!canAccept) {
   271→            // B is busy — log the rejection and let A fall back to idle/wander
   272→            if (simState?.pushEvent) {
   273→              simState.pushEvent({
   274→                type:           'talk_rejected',
   275→                initiatorLabel: character.label,
   276→                targetLabel:    target.label,
   277→                reason:         target.action,
   278→              });
   279→            }
   280→            // A idles for the normal decision interval (fallback handled by Engine wander)
   281→            character.wanderTimer = this.decisionIntervalMs;
   282→            break;
   283→          }
   284→
   285→          // Release any previous object reservation before walking to talk
   286→          if (character.targetObjectId) {
   287→            const prevObj = objects.find(o => o.id === character.targetObjectId);
   288→            if (prevObj) {
   289→              prevObj.release(character.name);
   290→              if (simState?.pushEvent) {
   291→                simState.pushEvent({
   292→                  type:      'fallback',
   293→                  charLabel: character.label,
   294→                  reason:    'plan_changed',
   295→                  fromLabel: prevObj.label ?? prevObj.name,
   296→                  toLabel:   target.label,
   297→                });
   298→              }
   299→            }
   300→            character.targetObjectId = null;
   301→          }
   302→
   303→          // Request Phase: walk A to a tile adjacent to B.
   304→          // Arrival handler in Engine will start the shared talking state.
   305→          const adjTile = simState?.findAdjacentWalkable?.(Math.round(target.tx), Math.round(target.ty));
   306→          if (adjTile && character.moveTo(adjTile.tx, adjTile.ty)) {
   307→            // Store pending talk so Engine knows what to do on arrival
   308→            character.pendingTalkTarget   = target;
   309→            character.pendingTalkDialogue = decision.dialogue       || null;
   310→            character.pendingTalkResponse = decision.targetDialogue || null;
   311→          }
   312→        }
   313→        break;
   314→      }
   315→    }
   316→
   317→    // For talk actions, dialogue is held until both characters enter talking state.
   318→    if (decision.dialogue && decision.action !== 'talk') {
   319→      character.currentDialogue = decision.dialogue;
   320→      character.dialogueTimer   = 5000;
   321→    }
   322→
   323→    if (decision.description) {
   324→      console.log(`[${character.label}] ${decision.description}`);
   325→    }
   326→
   327→    if (this.onDecision) {
   328→      this.onDecision(character, decision, objects, simState);
   329→    }
   330→  }
   331→}
   332→

The real solution is to prevent `_applyDecision` from executing while a character is actively interacting.\n\nWriting the guard logic... Still writing the fixes... Adding defensive cleanup logic... Then `_startConversation(charA, charB)` calls `charA.startTalk(charB, duration)` with no issues since `interactTarget` is already null.   "command": "gh pr create \\\n  --title \"fix: prevent stale slot reservations after character finishes interacting (FRG-229)\" \\\n  --body \"$(cat <<'EOF'\n## Summary\n\nFixes three distinct code paths that caused objects to stay permanently 'full' after a character finished interacting and left.\n\n- **Async AI race (primary cause):** `_applyDecision` could resolve between animation frames while a character was `interacting`, calling `moveTo()` and changing `action` to `'walking'` before the next frame's pre-update capture. The `prevAction === 'interacting'` detection then missed the transition entirely and the occupancy slot was never released. Fixed by guarding `_applyDecision` to discard stale decisions when character is already in `'interacting'` or `'talking'` state.\n- **Reservation leak via `_startConversation`:** When CharB was walking toward an object and became the target of a conversation, `startTalk()` cleared `targetObjectId` but never called `objectEngine.release()`, permanently orphaning the reservation in the object's `_reservations` set. Fixed by releasing CharB's pending reservation in `_startConversation` before entering the talking state.\n- **Defensive safety net:** Added a check at the top of the character loop \u2014 if `interactTarget` is set but `action !== 'interacting'`, logs a warning and releases immediately. Catches any future path that changes `action` without going through the normal end-of-interaction detection.\n\nAlso adds `console.warn` in `ObjectInstance.release()` when the charName is not a known occupant or reservation, making any future orphaned slots visible in the debug console.\n\n## Test plan\n\n- [ ] Run sim for 10+ sim hours and verify no object remains full after its character walks away\n- [ ] Verify stove, desk, easel, fridge, bonsai all return to available state after use\n- [ ] Check browser console: no `[Engine] defensive release` warnings during normal gameplay (confirms the async guard is working preventively)\n- [ ] Trigger a talk interruption mid-walk-to-object and verify the object slot is freed (no stale reservation)\n- [ ] QA re-verification pass\n\n\ud83e\udd16 Generated with [Claude Code](https://claude.com/claude-code)\nEOF\n)\""

USERMESSAGE #99
✓ TOOL RESULT
SUCCESS 
{"id":"8128823a-e372-42aa-9e64-acc0585ab0f1","identifier":"FRG-229","title":"Bug: Stale slot reservations — objects stay 'full' after character leaves","description":"## Problem

QA confirmed: objects show 'full' (occupied pip) permanently after characters finish interacting and leave. Stove showed 'full' for 8+ sim hours with no character present. Reproduced on stove, desk, easel, fridge, bonsai. Only Reset clears the stale slots.

## Evidence

* Stove: full from 2:40 PM onwards, no character at stove. Persisted until Reset.
* After Reset: Nyx used stove \\~10:12 AM, stove shows full at 1:46 PM with no character present.
* Bonsai: showed full for hours, eventually freed inconsistently.

## Root Cause

The interaction-end detection in Engine.js (line 108) checks prevAction === 'interacting' && char.action !== 'interacting' && prevInteractTarget, then calls objectEngine.release(). This SHOULD work but QA shows it doesn't reliably fire.

Possible causes:

1. The prevAction/prevInteractTarget capture (line 67-68) and char.update() (line 105) have a race — if something else changes the action between capture and check
2. arrive() is called with [char.name](<http://char.name>) but release() might use a different identifier
3. \\_handleObjectArrival clears targetObjectId before startInteraction — ordering issue with the detection
4. The object's auto_next timer might reset the state (and clear the interaction) BEFORE the character's interactTimer expires, breaking the detection

## Fix

Add defensive release: when a character transitions out of interacting (in Character.js or Engine.js), always release the slot. Add console.warn for any release on an unknown occupant to catch orphaned slots.

## Acceptance Criteria

* Objects return to correct free count after character finishes interaction
* No stale full pips after 10+ sim hours

ASSISTANTMESSAGE #102
## Status DONE ## What Changed - **`src/AIEngine.js`** — Guard `_applyDecision` to return early when `character.action` is `'interacting'` or `'talking'`. Prevents stale async LLM responses (resolved between rAF frames) from calling `moveTo()` and silently overriding the interacting state, which caused the occupancy slot to never be released. - **`src/Engine.js`** — Added defensive release at the top of the character loop: if `interactTarget` is set but `action !== 'interacting'`, log a warning and release the slot immediately (safety net for any future path that changes action without going through normal end-of-interaction detection). Also fixed `_startConversation` to release CharB's pending object reservation before entering the talking state (`startTalk()` was clearing `targetObjectId` without calling `objectEngine.release()`). - **`src/objects.js`** — Added `console.warn` to `ObjectInstance.release()` when the charName is not a known occupant or reservation, making any orphaned slots visible in the debug console. ## Key Decisions - **Async guard in `_applyDecision` rather than `moveTo`**: Guarding at the decision-application level is more explicit about intent — stale decisions are intentionally discarded, not silently swallowed. The held state still releases normally via its own timer. - **Defensive `interactTarget` check before `prevAction` capture**: Placed first in the character loop so it runs before anything else can use the stale state, and before `prevInteractTarget` is captured (ensuring the defensive release doesn't also trigger the detection below). ## PR / Branch - Branch: `feature/frg-229-fix-stale-slot-reservations` - PR: https://github.com/chillkimtest-oss/ai-aquarium-phaser/pull/13
